  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a707bdf3-9753-4d3b-a799-dd63e76e51a4'
      });

<div id="review_777526144" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/777526144" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/777526144?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer777526144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17289385277323220731"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473129427i/20412927.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475770202i/20764595.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To be honest here I was a little reluctant to start this series since I’m not really a fan of MC books. However, I’m happy to say <i>'Craving Constellation'</i>, the first installment in Nicole Jacquelyn’s series entitled <i>'The Aces'</i> was a total winner for me. It was raw, gritty, emotional and it sucked me in from the very beginning, but it also was sexy and passionate. Needless to say I enjoyed the hell out of it!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was the princess of Aces MC, and I had the bloody knuckles to prove it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Fiv</span>
  <span id="freeText17289385277323220731" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473129427i/20412927.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475770202i/20764595.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be honest here I was a little reluctant to start this series since I’m not really a fan of MC books. However, I’m happy to say <i>'Craving Constellation'</i>, the first installment in Nicole Jacquelyn’s series entitled <i>'The Aces'</i> was a total winner for me. It was raw, gritty, emotional and it sucked me in from the very beginning, but it also was sexy and passionate. Needless to say I enjoyed the hell out of it!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was the princess of Aces MC, and I had the bloody knuckles to prove it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Five years ago Brenna made a decision who changed her life irrevocably. Wanting to get away from the rough life she always lived, she chose to leave the MC life, the “Aces” where her father was the vice-president and make a life for herself somewhere else. She wanted something else, but now, five years later, realizing her new life it’s nothing like she had expected, she decides to run back to her old life, life had always been her only safe heaven. Brenna’s life for the last five years wasn’t exactly filled with hearts and flowers, living with an abusive husband being hard to say the least.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He was like a wounded animal, and I was the hunter who'd wounded him. I didn't know if he would ever forgive me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Dragon was just a new recruit five years ago when he met Brenna, at that time not knowing she is the VP’s daughter. He had been mesmerized by her beauty wanting more than anything to have her in his bed. After spending one hot, passionate night together, they part ways, Dragon never seeing Brenna again for five years. Five years it’s a long time, but Dragon never forget the redhead beauty or how strong their connection used to be.<br><br>When Dragon finds out Brenna is back and that she kept their daughter from him all these years he’s angry, confused, but as much as he wants to make the woman pay for everything, he can’t deny Brenna is a great mother or that he never stopped wanting her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It was like she was one of those sirens who lured men to their deaths.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475770202ra/20764596.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>'Craving Constellation'</i> was well written, consuming and I couldn’t put it down. The plot was well developed and while I found some aspects a little predictable, I enjoyed it! Both Brenna and Dragon were well developed characters. I liked Brenna for the most part, mainly because she was a great mother for her daughter, but I have to admit she pissed me off a couple of times. Also, the fact that she kept her daughter from Dragon for so many years was infuriating to say the least. She was well portrayed as a battered woman and overall she was an interesting character. <br><br>Dragon was more than I had expected to be honest. He was a mean douchebag with Brenna…at times, but he also was sweet, caring and very protective other times. I liked how he made her feel at some point – sexy and desirable and how honest he was with her about his intentions and feelings. I enjoyed how their tumultuous relationship between them progressed. Dragon knows from the start that he wants Brenna and their daughter and makes it clear numerous times. He was an alpha-male that I really liked reading about and I think he complemented our heroine pretty well. I also loved how his priorities started to change from the moment he finds out about his daughter. He loved her and cared for her from the moment he met her, their connection being palpable from the beginning. <br><br>Brenna and Dragon’s story is not only raw and gritty, but also steamy as hell. I loved all the sexy, passionate, explosive sex scenes between them and also Dragon’s dirty mouth. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He said it was gross, huh?” I said and raised my eyebrows. Then, I licked her pussy from her ass to her clit. Just like I remembered, it was sweet as fuckin’ candy. “Nope, not gross.” I licked her again.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475770202ra/20764597.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the supportive characters a lot! All of them were interesting and well portrayed and I’m looking forward to read their own stories. <br><br>All in all, <i>'Craving Constellations'</i> was a well written, emotional, gripping read and overall, a fantastic debut novel!<br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525702.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525703.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525705.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

This was definitely not a fluffy lighthearted read. Craving Constellations is everything you expect from a MC book. I felt so much while reading this book. Happy,sad and super pissed. This book hit nerves, left me raw and then made me swoon. <br><br><b> “You could gain fifty fuckin’ pounds, all that in your ass, and I’d still think you’re the sexiest woman I’ve ever seen,” he whispered before he leaned down and kissed me right above my left breast. “I love you, woman.”-Dragon</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Brenna%20Dragon_zpseqixmpar.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

She wants Dragon so she doesn't tell him who she is and sleeps with him. Not only do they have mind blowing sex but they stay up all night talking about everything. Tony is an abusive bastard and he beats her all the time. After 5 years she has had enough and she goes back to the life she ran from all those years ago. I really liked Brenna. I could understand where she was coming from for the most part. I will say that I think she was wrong for keeping Dragon's child from him, but I could understand not wanting a cheating biker for a man. I love that Brenna found the courage to leave her husband. Brenna's character presented a true representation of a battered wife. She felt very real. <br><br><b>“You want to know why I left?” My voice was wobbling, and I worked hard to control it. “I left because I was crazy about you, and I didn’t want to watch you fuck around. I left because I never wanted to hear that garbage you just spewed all over me.” He raised his eyebrows at me in surprise. “I left because I never wanted to watch you get hurt. I never wanted to visit you in prison. He is damn pissed that the one woman he wanted for 5 years not only left in the moring without a goodbye and never looked back, but she had his child and keep her from him for her whole life. Dragon was not your typical book hero. He could be mean as hell at times, but sweet too. He treats Brenna well for the most part and he loves her, but he is so hurt over the things she did to him that he lashes out and he doesn't hold back. At one point he crosses a line that was very hard to read. I'm not justifying his actions, but I did understand where he was coming from. <br><br><b>“You fuckin’ cunt! I love both Brenna and Dragon with Trix. Trix was absolutely adorable, and a daddy's girl from the minute she meets Dragon. One thing that really bugged me about the things that Brenna did was that she let her husband beat her so much that her daughter was scared to death to even breathe, I mean come on she may not want to be an old lady that gets cheated on but to let her daughter be around that. Why didn't she go home sooner? I just didn't get it. I really liked Poet, Brenna's dad. I know Poet has his own book and I am really looking forward to it. Over all this book was a great read that keep me on edge and reeling from emotional whiplash. I couldn't put it down. This is my first time reading Nicole Jacquelyn. I really enjoyed her writing style, and I can't wait to read more from her. <br><br><b>“I fuckin’ hate this shit, Brenna. I hate knowin’ he’s got any ties to either of ya. I fuckin’ hate that he can still make you fall to your knees in the yard like your legs ain’t got any strength left in ’em.   <i>“You could gain fifty fuckin’ pounds, all that in your ass, and I’d still think you’re the sexiest woman I’ve ever seen,” he whispered.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382365472i/5849579._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dragon</b>.. tall, full beard, long haired, dimpled, native american guy with tattoos on his knuckles. <b>100% ALPHA MALE!</b> <i>*gosh!*</i> I've read so many alpha males in my life but I will put him in my top 5 list. <i>(yep.. I have a list! lol!)</i> He's possessive, dominant, rough, talks dirty, orders you around, swears every fuckin' word and <b>I LOVE IT!!!!</b><br><br>One thing though.. and I think everyone will agree to me on this one.. a scene where he <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[hit Brenna.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/656143.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I COULDN'T BELIEVE IT!!! OMG.</b> I actually re-read it three times just to make sure I'm not seeing things.. but oh no.. he really did <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and it made me pissed!!! But after my pissy moment I understood where he was coming from and never been more glad that this one is a dual POV, as we get to see his emotions afterwards! I'm not saying what he did was right but that scene made his character feel more <b>REALISTIC.</b> The author satisfied me the way she redeemed him and come on.. it's a biker story! It's suppose to be <b>gritty</b> and <b>raw!</b> ^_^ <br><br>I usually favor one character over the other but I both LOVE Dragon and Brenna! <s>scratch</s> that, I love all the characters in this book! They are weird, fuck up crazy people! Reading them made me feel like I'm part of the gang. I think one of the reason why this book got me is because the characters felt so real.. <i>heck!</i> even the villains was so believable!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382366042i/5849859.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Craving Constellations</b> is intriguing, erotic, engaging, suspense, emotional, gritty with full alpha sexy men!<br><br>Sorry for my long "kinda" review! I cannot contain my emotions on this one. It's epic! I seriously cannot believe this is Nicole Jacquelyn first debut book. <br><br>I'm excited for Grease and Callie story!! &lt;3<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1510984496465295415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_710879349" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/710879349" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/710879349?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tissues-needed">tissues-needed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=books-with-an-edge">books-with-an-edge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=best-dirty-talk">best-dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=new-to-me-author">new-to-me-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710879349" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3375798323595876348"><b>4.5 Raw, gritty, and completely captivating stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879626._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>"I know, baby. I know you need control. But with me, you aren't gonna get it."</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879627._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>In my head I reminded myself that he was taken, but I couldn't get over the feeling that he had always been mine.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I went into this book with absolutely zero expectations. I'm a sucker for MC books, but after a recent string of very mediocre reads, I wasn't expecting much from a debut novel.<br/><br/>Holy shit was I wrong. This book blew me away! It was raw, gritty, painful,</span>
  <span id="freeText3375798323595876348" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Raw, gritty, and completely captivating stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879626._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"I know, baby. I know you need control. But with me, you aren't gonna get it."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879627._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>In my head I reminded myself that he was taken, but I couldn't get over the feeling that he had always been mine.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I went into this book with absolutely zero expectations. I'm a sucker for MC books, but after a recent string of very mediocre reads, I wasn't expecting much from a debut novel.<br><br>Holy shit was I wrong. This book blew me away! It was raw, gritty, painful, emotional, dark, passionate, and unputdownable until the very last page.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Five years ago Brenna made the decision to leave the only life she's ever known behind, in the hopes of building a different future for herself. Being the daughter of the vice president of a MC that runs guns is not exactly what she wants to be know for. What she doesn't expect is to run back to her old life when the new one she though she was building comes crumbling down on her. Leaving behind a brutally abusive husband, she takes her daughter and runs back to the only family she's ever been able to rely on.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879628._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Dragon is the Aces new lieutenant. When he first met Brenna at a club party he had just gotten his cut, and had no idea that the enticing woman that he felt such a pull to was his VP's daughter. They share a night of passion only for her to take off and then reappear in his life with one huge secret.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Fuckin’ gone for five years. No one hears from you. Now, you come back, and I find out you had my daughter and didn’t tell me FOR FIVE FUCKIN’ YEARS?".</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>Dragon is devasted that he was kept from his daughter for 4 years, and as much as he may blame Brenna for the decisions that she's made and her betrayal he can't seem to make himself stop wanting her.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879629.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nicole Jacquelyn took two imperfect and fucked up characters and wrote them in such a way that you just couldn't help but love them.<br><br>I am not typically a fan of heroines that are overly emotional but yet I felt for Brenna. Her life hasn't been an easy one, and although she has made some mistakes she still struggles to bring back the strong woman that she once was. She left behind her life because she didn't want to be the old lady on the sidelines while her man came home smelling like club whores. Dragon may not be perfect, but the magnetic pull between them is impossible for her to deny.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I went into the thing with Dragon looking for a little escape from reality, and I’d gotten way more than I bargained for. He wasn’t charming like Tony. He didn’t tell me sweet things. He was gruff and rude, and the things he said to me made me blush.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><br>Brenna and Dragon are attempting to mend things between them, but<br>will the secrets that she still hold on to threaten to break them once and for all?<br><br>Their relationship was gritty, painful, emotional, but real. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">We weren’t making love. It wasn’t sweet or soft. We were fucking, hard. Every movement was rough and needy, and for once, Dragon wasn’t talking me through it. We just needed to be as close as we possibly could before the world came tumbling around us again.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/668026.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved how the relationship between them, while having it's fair share of bumps and turns, felt real. Dragon may have been a rough around the edges, says what he wants with no holds barred Alpha man, but the way he felt pain broke my heart.<br><br>His pain bled through the pages to me. And even though Brenna was the sole reason behind this, I couldn't bring myself to blame her. They were both broken and tortured souls, and my heart went out for both of them.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He was like a wounded animal, and I was the hunter who'd wounded him. I didn't know if he would ever forgive me. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><br>There was a point in this book where Dragon did something that I would usually not be able to tolerate or understand in a hero. The fact that I not only forgave him for it, but understood his pain and remorse for it after the fact speaks volumes for the writing.<br><br>If you're looking for an emotionally charged, beautifully written MC book then you really need to give this one a try. I am really looking forward to the next book in this series (hopefully it will be Grease?)<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435412ra/879630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3375798323595876348" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_708099528" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/708099528" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/708099528?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708099528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2078462489778274665"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434968i/878423._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Craving Constellations is gritty, raw and fucking painful. Emotions bleed through the pages soaking everything in despair, longing and anger. Passion easily mix with rage, erotism with pain and love with hurt. </b><br/><br/>I think I’ve gone to heaven while reading Craving Constellations. This is the best example of what I love in MC Romance and I’m so happy I gave this book a chance! I didn’t have any expectations while I opened it and when I slowly started falling head over heels in love with this novel, I </span>
  <span id="freeText2078462489778274665" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434968i/878423._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Craving Constellations is gritty, raw and fucking painful. Emotions bleed through the pages soaking everything in despair, longing and anger. Passion easily mix with rage, erotism with pain and love with hurt. </b><br><br>I think I’ve gone to heaven while reading Craving Constellations. This is the best example of what I love in MC Romance and I’m so happy I gave this book a chance! I didn’t have any expectations while I opened it and when I slowly started falling head over heels in love with this novel, I couldn’t stop grinning! This story is dark, sexy and controversial.<br><br>This story starts with Brenna who is planing hers and her little daugther’s escape from abusive husband Anthony Richards. After 5 years of being together Brenna’s had enough of being beaten to bloody plump, she knows that her only chance of running away from her husband is coming back to her father, Poet who’s also MC’s Vice President. She’s afraid of coming back to bikers’ lifestyle and scared shitless of facing Dragon, the only man she’s been in love with and true father of her daugther. But she doesn’t have a choice. It’s better option to face her past than her husband’s merciless fist. <br><br>Ladies, meet Dragon. Dangerous, dominant and sexy as hell biker. He doesn’t know he has a daughter, he only spent one night with Brenna, night that made him want to make her his old lady and wife, so when he wakes up after the night of the best sex he’s ever had and she’s gone, he feels betrayed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434968i/878424._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dragon is fierce alpha male. I loved and hated this side of him. He’s full of sweet and panty melting moments, but also has darker side, and I don’t exactly know how I feel about it yet. He called Brenna almost every name in the book, along with cunt and was really agressive. I guess I could forgive him this, because Brenna never told him about his child so he has right to be angry with her. Dirty talking made me forget about it, though. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434968i/878425._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also loved how Dragon took care of his daugther, I swooned over him and his actions! There’s nothing sexier than rough man being gentle and caring for a child. Just wow. <br><br>I felt glued to the pages. It’s simply heartbreaking story with dark strike and amazingly hot sex. It has everything I am looking for in this type of romance. I’m so glad I picked it up.<br><br><i>More reviews on <a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Smokin' Hot Book Blog</a> and my <a href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Page</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2078462489778274665" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText2211673616124336046" style="display:none">3.5 This was a pretty good one!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419375574ra/13048192.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was a surprise, I admit.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_709328839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/709328839" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/709328839?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer709328839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13357832528587455688"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/>Reviewed for <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435166i/879134._SX540_.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, didn’t this book just tick the boxes. All I knew going into Craving Constellations was that it was it was based around a Motor Cycle Club….I’m badly craving my SOA fix so I thought “yeah, why not”.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>‘That was the best thing about this club and something I’d always craved growing up. You might fuck up, but the brothers wouldn’t ever act like you weren’t welcome. They’d punish you, but then it would be over, forgotten. You’d be back in the</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText13357832528587455688" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br><br>Reviewed for <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435166i/879134._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, didn’t this book just tick the boxes. All I knew going into Craving Constellations was that it was it was based around a Motor Cycle Club….I’m badly craving my SOA fix so I thought “yeah, why not”.<br><br><b>
  <i>‘That was the best thing about this club and something I’d always craved growing up. You might fuck up, but the brothers wouldn’t ever act like you weren’t welcome. They’d punish you, but then it would be over, forgotten. You’d be back in the fold.‘ </i>
</b>– Dragon<br><br>Whilst I may not have had any preconceived ideas about what to expect from Craving Constellations, I will say that anything I may have expected was exceeded. I loved this book. In theory, yes it’s a biker book, but it went deeper than that and dealt with so much more. This book elicited intense emotions from me, I loved the setting and I loved the humor and interactions between the guys in the club.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You really asking me about where I put my dick? Want to get a latte and fuckin’ gossip, too?” </i>
</b>- Dragon<br><br>My heart was racing in anticipation from the first page and I believed and felt every single little thread of emotion this author put into her story. I felt, believed it and, for the time I was consumed in this book, I lived it.<br><br><b>
  <i>“He was like a wounded animal, and I was the hunter who’d wounded him.” </i>
</b>- Brenna<br><br>I was ducking and diving through the pages and I reveled in twisting my way through the angst, the drama, the love, the pain, the freaking hot steamy sex, the violence and the absolute rawness of it all. No, it definitely wasn’t always pretty. In fact there was a time or two I felt darn right uncomfortable, a time or two I was bloody angry, but geez if there weren’t also those time when my heart melted, when I shed tears and times when I thought my heart would leap right out of my chest. I was unprepared for the level of emotion it would elicit.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I hated him, and I loved him at the same time, but mostly, I wanted to be able to take away the agony I saw on his face.” </i>
</b>- Brenna<br><br>Five years ago Brenna and Dragon shared a night of forbidden passion that not only seared their hearts and souls to one another but would result in decisions being made that could destroy them both. One night would fuse them, five years later the result of that night of passion and claiming would erupt into a love story borne of warmth and tenderness, coldness and violence, raw passion and desire, played out amidst chaos and mayhem, all in equal measures.<br><br><b>‘How many times had I dreamed of this? It was both a nightmare and a fantasy.’</b> - Brenna<br><br>I envisaged having a hard time believing the intensity of the feelings Dragon and Brenna would experience for one another after just one night, but believe it I did. I didn’t just believe it, I felt with every fibre of my being.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I knew what I needed to know. We were his. It was as terrifying and simple as that.” </i>
</b>- Brenna<br><br>Brenna, the daughter of Poet, the VP of Aces MC Club puts Dragon, a recent recruit in the club, at risk when she is overcome with passion after Dragon makes a move on her. It’s a unspoken rule that no one touches the club “Princess” - yet unfortunately for Dragon he has no idea who she is and Brenda doesn’t plan on sticking around for him to find out. Dragon feels an extreme level of lust towards Brenna and is drawn to her in so many ways.<br><br><b>
  <i>“It was like she was one of those sirens who lured men to their deaths.” </i>
</b> Dragon<br><br>Tough yet vulnerable Brenna leaves the safety of The Aces to start a new life. To leave the only life she has known and to escape the chaos and madness surrounding Aces Motorcycle Club.<br><br><b>
  <i>‘I wanted a husband who paid taxes and would take his car to a mechanic for routine maintenance. he wouldn’t get his hands dirty, wouldn’t raise his voice, and wouldn’t carry a gun.’</i>
</b> - Brenna<br><br>Brenna wants a life that doesn’t involve the day to day violence that has become her way of life at the Club. However, life didn’t go as planned for Brenna and after a five year absence she returns to the MC Club seeking refuge from an abusive marriage that has left both her and her little girl Trix scarred and fearing for their lives.<br><br><b>
  <i>“They were shrinking. Right in front of my eyes, my beautiful girls were pulling into themselves – as if they would disappear if they could just get small enough, quiet enough, still enough.” </i>
</b>- Dragon<br><br>Dragon knows nothing about Trix’s existence until he claps eyes her the day of Brenna’s return. Looking into the face very much like his own, Dragon knows this is his daughter, and this man, who has never known the love of a family outside of the club, is gutted that he’s missed out on so much of her life.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Fuckin’ gone for five years. No one hears from you. Now you come back and I find out you had my daughter and didn’t tell me. FOR FIVE FUCKIN’ YEARS.</i>
</b> - Dragon<br><br>But Brenna is harbouring other secrets that, when revealed, killed me. As did Dragons reactions to them. I felt both love and anger towards this strong, gorgeous, powerful alpha male. My feelings were so torn at one point and I was so angry I thought I would never get over it, but get over it I did. As I said, this story is raw and not always pretty. That’s not to say I condoned his actions because I didn’t, but the author did such a brilliant job of making me understand him, of making me feel for this conflicted man that I ended up judging the situation in the context of the whole story. As I said, I was pissed off with Dragon at the time, but I moved on and I came to understand and love this complex man who could show anger, love, pain, hurt, violence and kindness at the flip of a coin.<br><br><b>
  <i>“In my head, I reminded myself that he was taken, but I couldn’t get over the feeling that he had always been mine.” </i>
</b>– Brenna<br><br>Now, if I thought the beautiful interactions between Brenna and Trix melted my heart, then the scenes between Dragon and Trix were my undoing. This rough, hard, filthy mouthed man would become putty in the hands of this adorable and enchanting child. Each mesmerising scene would just melt me further. And the dance scene….wow! I was a complete gonner there. Just beautiful.<br><br><b>
  <i>“They were the most beautiful things I had ever seen in my entire goddam life, and they were worth every fuckin’ bruise I had.” </i>
</b>- Dragon<br><br>Dragon’s POV’s allowed me such an insight into this complex man and I relished every second I was inside his head. He may speak a little monosyllabic, but when he did have something to say, boy did he say it. There was no second guessing what was on Dragon’s mind but during those times when he felt so conflicted, seeing inside his head really did serve to help me understand him on another level and I really did need those insights. Oh and Dragon buddy…you can call me Mama any day…..swooooon.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I know, baby. I know you needed control. But with me, you aren’t gonna get it.”</i>
</b> – Dragon<br><br>Little Trix. Well, this child stole my heart. I ached for her and I loved her to pieces. I just wanted to pick her up and give her a huge Jenny hug. I adored this child and she stole every heartbreaking and heartwarming scene.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t believe you had my baby. She was all curled up in here, and I never saw it.” ……….”This is all I’ll ever see, Brenna. This is all I get. Let me look.”</i>
</b> – Dragon<br><br>So much happened in this story and I was completely and utterly riveted to every crazy moment. I devoured this book in one sitting and I eagerly await the next installment which I believe will be Grease’s story. Every character in this book has a story to tell and I hope we get to hear them all.<br><br>I loved the epilogue but I did find I wanted more. Craving Constellations was a heart stopping, temperature rising, angst inducing, emotional, gritty, raw, real and steamy hot read. Sign me up for more!!!! A fantastic debut novel from Nicole Jacquelyn which was beautifully written, flawlessly edited and one I didn’t want to end. Oh….and I’ll never be able to listen to Radioactive again without blushing…. ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="13357832528587455688" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15027112401194672546"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I really should stop re-reading*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Re-read: 05.04.2018</u>
</b><br/>I should have <i>not</i> have re-read this book. It started out fine, but then it just become too much.<br/>I didn't remember how badly <b>Brenna ‘Bren’ Richards</b> (27?) was treated, nor did I remember not liking <b>Daniel ‘Dragon’ White</b> so much. It was strange not feeling the story, nor the characters. I usually like - if not love - biker books, but this one just didn't feel <i>right</i> for me. I guess this is an obvious proof at how changed I have </span>
  <span id="freeText15027112401194672546" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I really should stop re-reading*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 05.04.2018</u>
</b><br>I should have <i>not</i> have re-read this book. It started out fine, but then it just become too much.<br>I didn't remember how badly <b>Brenna ‘Bren’ Richards</b> (27?) was treated, nor did I remember not liking <b>Daniel ‘Dragon’ White</b> so much. It was strange not feeling the story, nor the characters. I usually like - if not love - biker books, but this one just didn't feel <i>right</i> for me. I guess this is an obvious proof at how changed I have become, of how much more picky I am now than I was before.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I was the princess of the Aces MC, and I had the bloody knuckles to prove it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br>↦ <b>Bellatrix ‘Trix’ Colleen Richards</b> (4), Brenna and Dragon's daughter. <br>↦ <b>Anthony ‘Tony’ Richards</b>, Brenna's abusive husband.<br>↦ <b>Poet</b>, belonged to the Aces MC; was the vice president. He's also Brenna's dad.<br>↦ <b>Grease</b>, a cut member of Aces motorcycle club.<br>↦ <b>Casper</b>, a recruit for Aces motorcycle club.<br>↦ <b>Slider</b>, the president of Aces motorcycle club, and his old lady, <b>Vera</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I’d never imagined the world I chose would be far worse than the one I had left.</i>
  </b>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522895690ra/25327223.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Abuse?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, Brenna got abused by her husband and Dragon hits her once. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Bellatrix ‘Trix’ Colleen Richards.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - No.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Unsure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Not again.<br><b>New Rating</b> - 2.5 stars.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br>I like it.<br><b>Rate: 3.5 stars. </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_709567486" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/709567486" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/709567486?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=second-chance-romance">second-chance-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer709567486" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6023101739981139804"><b>I LOVE THIS BOOK!!! <br/>And woohoo!! A brand new biker series for me to obsess over!</b><br/><br/>The first book in <i>The Aces</i> series tells the story of biker Princess, Brenna. Her father is the Vice President of The Aces MC, and she grew up surrounded by the violence, shady practices and non-traditional relationships of the club. Having decided that that isn’t what she wants her life to be, she ran away from the lifestyle after College, and married a straight, ‘safe’ man who instead turned out to be an abusively v</span>
  <span id="freeText6023101739981139804" style="display:none"><b>I LOVE THIS BOOK!!! <br />And woohoo!! A brand new biker series for me to obsess over!</b><br /><br />The first book in <i>The Aces</i> series tells the story of biker Princess, Brenna. Her father is the Vice President of The Aces MC, and she grew up surrounded by the violence, shady practices and non-traditional relationships of the club. Having decided that that isn’t what she wants her life to be, she ran away from the lifestyle after College, and married a straight, ‘safe’ man who instead turned out to be an abusively violent asshole. Five years later she and her four year old daughter make a desperate escape from their nightmare with nowhere else to go but to return to her father and the only home she has ever truly known. <br /><br />Of course that brings her back to Dragon. Brenna’s run from the MC had a lot to do with Dragon after they shared one very hot and steamy night together on the night of his initiation into the club. He didn’t know who she was at the time (she never told him, knowing that she was off limits to the boys), and, assuming he would never give her the kind of relationship that she wanted with him, she left the following morning, never seeing him again. And upon her arrival back at the compound, Dragon not only sees the one woman he has never been able to forget, but he takes one look at her daughter and recognizes her as his own. <br /><br />The book is dual POV so we get to see everything that is going on between Brenna and Dragon and it’s absolutely sensational! They still have strong feelings for each other, and being thrown back together in such intense circumstances brings the emotion straight to boiling point.<br /><br /><i>“Fuckin’ gone for five years. No one hears from you. Now, you come back, and I find out you had my daughter and didn’t tell me FOR FIVE FUCKIN’ YEARS?” His voice was steadily rising, and by the time he finished, he was roaring in my face.</i><br /><br />Brenna had her reasons for doing what she did, and even though I was initially angry with her, as her story unfolded I could see why she thought she was doing the right thing. Dragon is justifiably pissed with her, but he still wants her, and he is quick to make his feelings known. <br /><br />“<i>Yeah, okay, Brenna. You wanna pretend like you and me aren’t what we are, that’s fine. I’m not gonna pretend. I’m not takin’ your bullshit either. Baby, I’ve been waitin’ five years for you. That shit’s never gone away. So, you can bitch and moan and make your own life miserable, or you can suck it the fuck up and get on the same page with me. I’m not goin’ anywhere.</i>”<br /><br />Aaaaahhh, you’ve gotta love him!<br /><br />But in the five years that she has been away, Brenna has endured more than anybody knows. Having lived in fear, she is not the carefree, confident young girl that she once was, and one of the things I loved about this story was watching Brenna relax in the comfort of her new family, and start to find herself again. Thanks to a bit of help from her man. <br /><br /><i>“I was looking forward to fuckin’ the Stepford wife right out of her.”</i><br /><br />I love Dragon! A totally alpha biker, he is incredibly devoted to his family, and clearly in love with Brenna, determined to help her heal from all that she has been through. He is also totally sexy with a filthy, filthy mouth!<br /><br /><i>Before I could take another breath, she’d taken me to the root.<br /></i>“Shit!”<i><br />“I’m sorry!” She looked at me, her eyes wide, as she tried to scramble off me.<br />“Brenna, if you get up, I’ll fuckin’ spank your ass! Fuckin’ ride me, woman!”</i><br />	<br />Yep, there’s a whole lot of sexy time going on, and it’s really freaking HOT!!!! The love story between Brenna and Dragon is absolutely gorgeous, with never any doubt that these two belong together, and the sex is an important part of that. And despite all of the history between them, and the lifestyle that they live in, they are actually fairly functional together. <br /><br />Of course there are some ups and downs, and things get VERY intense as the past comes roaring back into their lives. There are some shocks, and I actually gasped out loud a couple of times. One scene in particular left me gaping with my mouth open, but the author does a fantastic job of getting us into the heads of both Brenna and Dragon. The emotion in just those few scenes, and the impact that it has on the characters absolutely broke my heart!! There is so much pain! It was awful, but so amazingly written! But even with this most unexpected blip in their reunion, I could understand and empathise with what they were going through, at no time did I feel the need to hurl my kindle, and that’s always a positive thing! The bottom line is – the love each other! They made mistakes, they made up for it, they moved on. And I loved it!<br /><br />This book isn’t as gritty as some of the other biker series out there. There isn’t much of a focus on the activities on the club, or the seedier side of the lifestyle. It’s there, but it doesn’t really impact on what is going on between Brenna and Dragon. They are both so incredibly committed to each other, and to little Trix (who is all kinds of awesome!). I also loved the wider MC family, and how they form such a tight knit community who, without question, have each other’s backs. <br /><br />This is a really short book, and the story is well paced, moving quickly. I adored Brenna and Dragon’s story, and was enthralled from start to finish, feeling every emotion right alongside them right up to the ending that had my heart pounding, and the gorgeous, cliffy free HEA left me smiling like an idiot.<br /><br /><i>“I love you, woman.”<br />“Love you, too,” I replied with a smile...<br />“Now, kiss your man.” </i><br /><br />There are a few threads left undone, and a couple of possible storylines are set up for future books – particularly for Grease and Caspar. I can’t wait for the next in the series. <br /><br />I absolutely loved it!<br /><br />4.5 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6023101739981139804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Angie **loves angst**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3069040-angie-loves-angst"><img alt="Angie **loves angst**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438103550p2/3069040.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/708434247?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie **loves angst**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie **loves angst**" href="/user/show/3069040-angie-loves-angst">Angie **loves angst**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708434247" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10352201849044818530"><blockquote>
  <b>"Doing the thing you know is best doesn't make it less scary."</b>
</blockquote><br/>When a book is labeled MC, its like I'm a magnet drawn to it, and I have no choice but to pause what I'm reading and get right to it.<br/><br/><b>Brenna</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"How much could a person take before she completely fell apart?"</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435028i/878610.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Dragon</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435028i/878611.jpg' width='350' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800287i/667095.png' width='400' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Tired of being her husband's punching bag for five years Brenna packs up her stuff and runs away. She goes for shelter to her father who is the Vice-President of the Aces MC. Upon returning home Brenna has to face the lif</span>
  <span id="freeText10352201849044818530" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Doing the thing you know is best doesn't make it less scary."</b>
</blockquote><br>When a book is labeled MC, its like I'm a magnet drawn to it, and I have no choice but to pause what I'm reading and get right to it.<br><br><b>Brenna</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>"How much could a person take before she completely fell apart?"</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435028i/878610.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dragon</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435028i/878611.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800287i/667095.png" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Tired of being her husband's punching bag for five years Brenna packs up her stuff and runs away. She goes for shelter to her father who is the Vice-President of the Aces MC. Upon returning home Brenna has to face the life she's left behind, along with the man, Dragon, she left behind. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"I told myself I was running to my Pop, but I wasn't. I was running to Dragon the same way I had always run to him in my mind when I needed him."</b>
</blockquote><br>Five years ago, after one night of hot, sweaty sex Brenna ran away from Dragon without telling him who she was. Their night of passion caused life-changing circumstances that all comes to light with Brenna's return home. Dragon was understandably a douche in the beginning because of a huge secret that Brenna has kept from him. They never really got to know each other or start a relationship.This book focussed on Brenna and Dragon starting and rebuilding their relationship. <br><br>***Dragon did something in this book that was an absolute deal breaker for me, especially considering Brenna's past. He should have known and done better. Even though I felt his regret and sincere apology that was just a definite <i>no/never</i> for me.***<br><br>By the end of the book I felt that Brenna and Dragon truly did love each other and their hea was very sweet. I enjoyed the family connection that the club shared. Everyone was there to support and help, Brenna but they were also sure to let her know that she messed up.<br><br>I really enjoyed this, but I felt that it was a bit too predictable. I will definitely read this author's work again, and I'm hoping some of the other members in the club get their own books. I would recommend this book to those of you who enjoy MC books and may be looking for a quick read.<br><br><b>Rating: 3.5 Second Chance Love Stars</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11244854570350421131"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387369929ra/7585047.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If there was nothing else about this book that bothered me, the fact that Dragon hit Brenna, is enough to make this a NOPE book for me. You can try to rationalize it all you want, but a man that is so out of control that he hits the woman he supposedly loves, is not a safe man to be with. I don't care if he feels badly afterward. Game over. <br/><br/>Unfortunately, there was plenty more that bothered me about this, but for the sake of this review, let's just limit it to interactions between Brenna and Dra</span>
  <span id="freeText11244854570350421131" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387369929ra/7585047.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If there was nothing else about this book that bothered me, the fact that Dragon hit Brenna, is enough to make this a NOPE book for me. Game over. <br><br>Unfortunately, there was plenty more that bothered me about this, but for the sake of this review, let's just limit it to interactions between Brenna and Dragon. <br>1. He chokes her in anger<br>2. Ge calls her a c*nt and bitch<br>3. He tells her what to wear and how to do her hair<br>4. He yells at her<br>5. He dictates what she will put up with and tells her how things will be<br>6. He tells her that he's the one "in control" and she needs to accept that<br>7. and of course, HE HITS HER <br><br>Basically Brenna goes from one abusive relationships to another. This is not a romance. </span>

<div id="review_1220291850" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1220291850" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1220291850?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1220291850" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14035228747747170116"><b>4 MC, Star Gazing, Soul-Searching Stars</b><br/><br/>At first I didn’t know this was an MC book. Judging by the cover, I thought this would be a sappy NA romance novel. I’m completely taken aback and the reviews make sense.<br/><br/>This book has a lot of mixed reviews. Some loved it and some liked it, but it left them feeling odd. I totally get this now.<br/><br/>I love MC books. Of course they start to blur a bit, but it’s the plot that makes the stories unique and gripping. When I read a MC book I always take myself into that</span>
  <span id="freeText14035228747747170116" style="display:none"><b>4 MC, Star Gazing, Soul-Searching Stars</b><br><br>At first I didn’t know this was an MC book. Judging by the cover, I thought this would be a sappy NA romance novel. I’m completely taken aback and the reviews make sense.<br><br>This book has a lot of mixed reviews. Some loved it and some liked it, but it left them feeling odd. I totally get this now.<br><br>I love MC books. Of course they start to blur a bit, but it’s the plot that makes the stories unique and gripping. When I read a MC book I always take myself into that world. The guys kill, cheat, steal and there’s no laws or rules. You grit your teeth at some of the stuff, but you secretly crave it because it’s so darn good to read!<br><br><b>Summary</b><br><br>Brenna is escaping from her ex-husband. He has been abusing her for five years and she finally can leave him. She has a baby-girl and it’s not his (he is aware of this). She’s running to her dad, who is VP of a MC.<br><br>Brenna’s daughter looks nothing like Brenna or her ex. She looks exactly like Dragon and when Dragon sees his daughter for the first time, he knows she is his.<br><br><b>Brenna and Dragon</b><br><br>You feel for Brenna and Dragon. Brenna did a crappy thing. She had sex with Dragon and didn’t tell him she is the VP’s daughter and then after she finds out she’s knocked up, she doesn’t tell him. It took me awhile to get over it. I had to really dig deep and see it from her POV.<br><br>Then Dragon’s reaction towards Brenna is very MC like. He’s very harsh, mean, arrogant and very domineering. I’m usually a huge fan of this, but Dragon rubbed me the wrong way. If you have read the book, then you know what I am talking about. <br><br>I’m not sure that I’m fully convinced Dragon could be a Hero to me. I felt like there should be a little more redemption on his part, but that is me.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>The love story is crazy, intense, raw and it’s simply that. A love story. Craving Constellation has so many mixed reviews because the book is a touch taboo and really emotional. I really wanted to love it, but I couldn’t get over some parts.<br><br>I did love the daughter, but I’m always a sucker for kids in books, so that’s just me.<br><br>If you are a MC fan, this is a good one to read. It won’t be easy, there’s some crazy stuff that happens, but you won’t be disappointed. <br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17859911.Craving_Constellations__The_Aces___1_" title="Craving Constellations (The Aces, #1) by Nicole Jacquelyn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1377563339s/17859911.jpg" alt="Craving Constellations (The Aces, #1) by Nicole Jacquelyn" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://amzn.to/18XPGll" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a> Also on Kindle Unlimited</span>
  <a data-text-id="14035228747747170116" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <b>
    <i> Baby, I’ve been waitin’ five years for you. That shit’s never gone away. So, you can bitch and moan and make your own life miserable, or you can suck it the fuck up and get on the same page with me. I’m not goin’ anywhere.</i>

Married </span>
  <span id="freeText4466979279977684097" style="display:none"><i>5 stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Baby, I’ve been waitin’ five years for you. That shit’s never gone away. So, you can bitch and moan and make your own life miserable, or you can suck it the fuck up and get on the same page with me. I’m not goin’ anywhere.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385347167i/7130392._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ever hear of the saying out of the pot and into the fire, well that is exactly what Brenna did, <b>Princess of the Aces MC</b> broke one of the club rules and scared of the outcome, she turned her back on the world she grew up and went on the road to hell. Married to a monster in a suit, she’s had enough of being used as a human punching bag, she has one shot to be free, and that means coming home and facing everything she left behind.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You want to know why I left?” My voice was wobbling, and I worked hard to control it. “I left because I was crazy about you, and I didn’t want to watch you fuck around. I left because I never wanted to hear that garbage you just spewed all over me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385347167i/7130393._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For five years Dragon’s been waiting for her to come back, but never expected all the baggage she brought along with her, all the secrets, all the lies, it’s time to right the wrongs even if it means getting the shit beat out of him.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>They were the most beautiful things I had ever seen in my entire goddamn life, and they worth every fuckin’ bruise I had.</i>
  </b>

She knows the life of a Princess, but could only guess what it would be like as an Old Lady, but Dragon happily proved her wrong and she realizes that this is a life worth livin... the only thing that matters is having the people who love you right at your side. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I was looking forward to fuckin’ the Stepford wife right out of her.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385347167ra/7130395.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brenna’s husband isn’t a man to fuck with, he has many powerful connections that can cause all sorts of trouble for the Aces MC, but the man in the suit doesn’t know how far her family will stick together and protect their own.<br><br>This is a book you just gotta live in, it’s fucked up but damn is it beautiful! Dragon was a delicious alpha-biker and Brenna was a strong woman who really grew from the young naive girl who ran away when she was scared. I wish I can say more, but I can't, it wouldn't be fair to you. All the characters in the story you just wanted to devour and read more about, especially Ghost, I hope we'll get his story one day. <br><br>I am seriously kicking myself for waiting so long to read this book, I’ve had it for quite some time and I am so happy I picked it up that one lonely night, the only problem was I started it close to midnight so I pretty much was a walking zombie the next day, but it was totally worth it! I can’t wait for more, up next is Grease and Callie’s story which proves to be just as exciting as this one. <br></span>

<div id="review_709529100" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/709529100" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/709529100?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer709529100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5646243062618835123">To enter a book with absolutely no expectations and then have those expectations punch you right in the face. To have those expectations bend you over a table and make you feel things in all the right places. Damn...it's a beautiful thing. <br/><br/><i>Craving Constellations</i> was a beautiful thing.<br/><br/>Beautifully raw and hard.<br/><br/>Beautifully emotional and real.<br/><br/>Anyone who knows me, knows how I feel about insta-love. It's an insta-turnoff. I like things to build, I like tension. Tease me, torture me; don't give it to m</span>
  <span id="freeText5646243062618835123" style="display:none">To enter a book with absolutely no expectations and then have those expectations punch you right in the face. To have those expectations bend you over a table and make you feel things in all the right places. Damn...it's a beautiful thing. <br /><br /><i>Craving Constellations</i> was a beautiful thing.<br /><br />Beautifully raw and hard.<br /><br />Beautifully emotional and real.<br /><br />Anyone who knows me, knows how I feel about insta-love. It's an insta-turnoff. I like things to build, I like tension. Tease me, torture me; don't give it to me quick. But damn if Nicole Jacquelyn just made me insta-eat-my-own-words. She pulled it off, and pulled me in. <br /><br />Brenna and Dragon pulled me in. This is not your typical MC romance. It has everything you love about a good MC book, but it had more....more; it had more heart. It pushed the limits, but knew when to pull back. Sometimes we <i>do</i> want a book to emotionally rake us over the coal, but sometimes we just want to experience the emotion. Experience it <i>without</i> breaking. I didn't break; I felt.<br /><br />Lately I've been seeing a lot of author bashing because of content. Readers thinking authors are taking the alpha male behavior a little too far. Toeing the line of abuse. Do they? Sometimes, maybe, but they are attacking these authors for condoning this behavior. News flash my people, just because an author writes about it, doesn't mean they condone it. <br /><br />Just because an author writes about rape, doesn't mean they're ready to fund the next kickstarter project supporting the rapists of America. Americans feed on drama. Even if we don't want to admit it, we feed on pain. We feed off these insane worlds where wrong, seems so right. We open wide and beg to be fed. <br /><br />I think that's what I loved about this book. I was fed, boy was I fed!!<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews@gmail.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews@gma...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5646243062618835123" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer10870064333525046217"><br/><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>This book was actually very easy to rate. There were parts of it that I "liked" (3 stars) and parts that I "really liked" (4 stars) so <i>my</i> overall rating is 3.5 which is pretty good for a debut novel and a genre that so many authors out there manage to attempt & fuck up in the process.<br/><br/>What can I say? When a guy also happens to have a motorcycle between his legs, you don't have to twist my arm to get me to at least try the book. This one was good enough for me to finish. It was a quick re</span>
  <span id="freeText10870064333525046217" style="display:none"><br /><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />This book was actually very easy to rate. There were parts of it that I "liked" (3 stars) and parts that I "really liked" (4 stars) so <i>my</i> overall rating is 3.5 which is pretty good for a debut novel and a genre that so many authors out there manage to attempt &amp; fuck up in the process.<br /><br />What can I say? When a guy also happens to have a motorcycle between his legs, you don't have to twist my arm to get me to at least try the book. This one was good enough for me to finish. It was a quick read, the writing was decent, the story had a couple of "huh??" moments but good overall so, all in all, I enjoyed it.<br /><br />I would recommend this book if you enjoy stories about MC lifestyle that: 1. aren't overly crude, 2. where sexual content is present but doesn't define the book &amp; 3. the story has substance to it.<br /><br />I am definitely looking forward to reading more books in this series &amp; from this author in general.<br /><br />Cheers!</span>
