<div id="review_709010890" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/709010890" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/709010890?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer709010890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5456723309621730868"><b>4.5 MC, Dirty Talkin', Smokin' Hero, Fast Reading Stars<br/>* * * * 1/2</b><br/>Since joining GoodReads, one of the types of books I have found really entertaining has been the MC story-line. It may be due to my never having experienced anything close to that type of environment or just a like of the "bad boy on a bike" story that captures my attention.<br/><br/>I share this as a backdrop to my take on Craving Constellations. This story started out strong from the get go. We are in the head of Brenna, as she plots to l</span>
  <span id="freeText5456723309621730868" style="display:none"><b>4.5 MC, Dirty Talkin', Smokin' Hero, Fast Reading Stars<br />* * * * 1/2</b><br />Since joining GoodReads, one of the types of books I have found really entertaining has been the MC story-line. It may be due to my never having experienced anything close to that type of environment or just a like of the "bad boy on a bike" story that captures my attention.<br /><br />I share this as a backdrop to my take on Craving Constellations. This story started out strong from the get go. We are in the head of Brenna, as she plots to leave a horrific situation, think Julia Roberts Sleeping with the Enemy bad. She has figured out how to leave this marriage with her 4 year old daughter without a trace, returning to where she thought she had escaped so many years ago, The Aces. <br /><br />Brenna was the Princess of the club. Growing up and seeing what biker life was she decided long ago, she wanted more. She wanted not to be an "Old Lady"; not to think about sharing a man, smelling others on him when he came home and not wondering if the man she loved was going to be locked up. She wanted to feel safe and protected. She thought the outside world would give her that. She had a rude awakening. <br /><br />She returns to the club knowing she is in for the hardest confrontation of her life. She has broken all of the rules the club believes in and has to ask for her father to take her in. Oh, there just a couple of other things to deal with... she slept with a brother in the club without telling him she was the VP's daughter, takes off then discovers she is pregnant. She marries the crazy politically connected guy and lets 5 years go by before finally being able to escape and come home. <br /><br />Needless to say the real father of her child, Dragon, was not pleased finding out he missed out on the first five years of his daughter's life.<br /><br />Time out: <br />You should read this book just for Dragon. He has a back story and a sweet yet still very strong presence. I'm just sayin', you'll like the Dragon, I know I did. sigh<br />And back...<br /><br />This is the set up and I do not want to give you anymore than this. Why you ask?<br /><br />Because. The. Book. Is. That. Damn. Good. <br /><br />This book doesn't pretend to be anything but what it is. It has really strong plot points. The lead characters are drawn so you feel you have a sense of who they are and their emotions. All of the supporting players are part of the story and not thrown in for filler. There are twists and no cliffy. Are there more intense biker books out there, yes; But the book was just right for me and if you give yourself to this fast engrossing read, you will not be disappointed. I know I wasn't.<br /><br />Nicole Jacquelyn put grit, steam, family ties and heart together and tied it all up in a MC book. I will look for her next book and click click without hesitation. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5456723309621730868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_735133665" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/735133665" />
    <a title="Vallsykes" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes"><img alt="Vallsykes" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367067514p2/5164414.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/735133665?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vallsykes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vallsykes" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes">Vallsykes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Biker Romance Lovers- &amp; if you love emotional reads!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=ptsd">ptsd</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=been-there-read-that">been-there-read-that</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=more-than-3-stars">more-than-3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=too-little-too-late">too-little-too-late</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=multiple-or-dual-pov">multiple-or-dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=wtf-conflict">wtf-conflict</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=can-t-believe-his-mouth">can-t-believe-his-mouth</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=motorcycle-club">motorcycle-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=separation-plot">separation-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer735133665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6500639462176547333"><b>3.5 stars</b> <i>I keep wavering between 3 and 4 stars...but in general, it was a <b>typical story made noteworthy</b> by the style of writing,</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381094740i/4173919._SX540_.jpg' width='280' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>After reading this book, I thought of the song, <b>"Starlight" by Muse</b>: <blockquote>
  <i>Far away <br/> The ship is taking me far away <br/> Far away from the memories <br/> Of the people who care if I live or die <br/><br/> The starlight <br/> I will be chasing a starlight <br/> Until...I don't know if it's worth it anymore</i>
</blockquote>Despite knowing there is a separation plot and having a pet peeve about heroines who keep secret</span>
  <span id="freeText6500639462176547333" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b> <i>I keep wavering between 3 and 4 stars...but in general, it was a <b>typical story made noteworthy</b> by the style of writing,</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381094740i/4173919._SX540_.jpg" width="280" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After reading this book, I thought of the song, <b>"Starlight" by Muse</b>: <blockquote>
  <i>Far away <br> The ship is taking me far away <br> Far away from the memories <br> Of the people who care if I live or die <br><br> The starlight <br> I will be chasing a starlight <br> Until...I don't know if it's worth it anymore</i>
</blockquote>Despite knowing there is a separation plot and having a pet peeve about heroines who keep secret babies from the heroes(because there is almost never a great explanation for it), I will say that Craving Constellations was an interesting read. The writer had me raising my eyebrows at how she portrayed the heroine, Brenna. <br><br>Brenna is a woman who ran away from what she thought she didn't want or need, only to get caught in a marriage from hell! Here, I wish the author would have had Brenna "get a clue" faster than she did. I wish that Brenna would have continued to use her "keen" judgment after she'd made the decision that the biker life wasn't for her, but no. Instead she turned into some warped Stepford wife of an abusive sociopath. And it takes five years for her to go running home to her biker family with her tail between her legs.<br><br>The plot goes predictably: Brenna seeks sanctuary and confesses to the horrors of her marriage; then the brothers(which include her father)are brimming with the fire of revenge. In the midst of all that is Dragon, the club member who Brenna spent one forbidden wild night with. Even though Brenna kept a huge secret from him and more, Dragon gets rid of his current old lady, and he and Brenna become an insta-family **<i>rolls eyes</i>**...I wasn't amused.<br><br>Yet, it's the conversations and inner thoughts that fill up the plot sequence that intrigued me the most. No doubt, everyone feels, on some level, betrayed by Brenna's leave of absence. Brenna has to bear the shame and guilt of her misjudgment, secrets and failure to contact her loved ones, even during necessary times. And she isn't easily forgiven, nor does the mark of her betrayal and bad decisions go away too soon. Brenna grows and changes, and though some of her actions make no sense, she narrowly escapes the label of "weak" or "trippy", IMO. <br><br>More interestingly, the fact that the club, Brenna's father, and Dragon were not without fault is what brought things full circle. It becomes the "shoulda, woulda, coulda" game, and throughout the first 80%, I was engrossed in the complicated feelings shared between Brenna &amp; her father(Poet), Brenna &amp; Dragon, Dragon &amp; Poet, etc., that bordered love &amp; hate and resided in the gray area of acceptance, forgiveness and ...just plain-- hurt.<blockquote>
  <i>Hold you in my arms <br> I just wanted to hold <br>You in my arms <br><br> My life <br> You electrify my life <br> Let's conspire to ignite <br> All the souls that would die just to feel alive <br> <br>Our hopes and expectations <br> Black holes and revelations</i>
</blockquote>The writing captured my attention, with some memorable conversations and rather poignant streams of consciousness.<br><br>Conversely, I must say that some thoughts of the characters, especially Brenna, were in danger of being repetitive. The greater, outside threat(Brenna's soon-to-be-ex husband who got away with way too much) wasn't developed very well, which made the last 20% seem rushed. Overall, a lot of things go unexplained. For example: Dragon's PoV is missing at very crucial turns. His pain is talked about, but I couldn't perceive it because we don't get as much of his background as we get of Brenna's. Also, he and Brenna had only spent one night together, so their whole connection is a bit "missed". The author tries to give them a connection with a shared interest(really it's Brenna's interest)in constellations, but honestly Brenna and Dragon go at it like they'd known each other for years. I'm supposed to believe they shared <u>everything (sex, love, hopes and dreams)</u> in one night?!**<i>rolling eyes</i>** A night where Dragon had no idea who Brenna's father was, who Brenna really was?.[<i>I just didn't feel great chemistry between the two, initially, based on how their relationship is started. But it gets better later in the story.</i>.]<br><br>The story was good and readers will no doubt like that it's a decent Biker Romance(though not too much Biker action went on). However, I was more caught by the author's potential for creating situations that are "read" worthy, despite some shortcomings, and I'd like to think that the potential will grow. I will try the next installment of the Aces series. <br><br><b>WARNING:</b> the hero betrays the heroine in a "not cool" way; it's just as bad as cheating. It happens once, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he backhands her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>,and there is a multi-layered context that stems from the heroine's own betrayal to explain it[but not excuse it], but it's a horrible moment just the same.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6500639462176547333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15696756160698212572">09/04/2013 --<br/><b><br/>Overall Rating = 2.5 Stars<br/>Book Cover / Book Blurb / Book Title = 3 / 3 / 5 = 3.5 Stars<br/>Writer’s Voice = 3 Stars<br/>Character Development = 3 Stars<br/>Story Appreciation = 3.5 Stars<br/>Worth the Chili = 1 Star </b>-- [$2.99 on Amazon for a debut Indie book!]<br/><br/><b>I liked this book, but there were issues. Let me tell you what I liked first:</b><br/><br/>1 -- This is a debut book by this author [this will come again later]. For a debut book, it was okay. There really was nothing unique here, but what we did have was an en</span>
  <span id="freeText15696756160698212572" style="display:none">09/04/2013 --<br /><b><br />Overall Rating = 2.5 Stars<br />Book Cover / Book Blurb / Book Title = 3 / 3 / 5 = 3.5 Stars<br />Writer’s Voice = 3 Stars<br />Character Development = 3 Stars<br />Story Appreciation = 3.5 Stars<br />Worth the Chili = 1 Star </b>-- [$2.99 on Amazon for a debut Indie book!]<br /><br /><b>I liked this book, but there were issues. Let me tell you what I liked first:</b><br /><br />1 -- This is a debut book by this author [this will come again later]. For a debut book, it was okay. There really was nothing unique here, but what we did have was an enjoyable few hours. There weren't huge editing issues and we all know that's a plus. Saying this, I'll also stress again, there was nothing unique. You could choose not to read it and not miss much.<br /><br />2 -- The characters were fairly well developed. A few things didn't add up, but they didn't annoy me. This is one of my personal pet peeves -- does the story make sense and once developed, do the characters act in character. For this component, I give it 3 Stars. Just okay.<br /><br />3 -- I loved the title of this book. It intrigued me and once I read the book, it made total sense.<br /><br /><b>Okay, now for those items I wasn't crazy about:</b><br /><br />1 -- This is a debut Indie author. I think the price point is high. I used my Prime membership and got this on loan for August. I wouldn't pay $3 unless others told me there was something I was missing by not reading this. Let me say it again, if you choose not to read this book, you won't miss anything you haven't read before -- probably better.<br /><br />I think this is a case of putting either a motorcycle on the cover or in the blurb and watching them swarm. So, you have been WARNED!!<br /><br />**spoiler alert**<br /><br />2 -- Brenna loves her Dad. She loved people in the Ace's MC. Then, she just walked away. Without a backwards glance, she just walked away. This does not make sense to me. The author didn't do a good job with this one.<br /><br />3 -- Brenna was beaten severely by her husband and leave him. She runs to Dad and finds Dragon again. Dragon and she have a misunderstanding and he backhands her. She is fine with this. This so does not jive with my concept of a healthy relationship. No reason. None. I. DO. NOT. LIKE. HOW. THIS. AUTHOR. HANDLES. THIS. Not at all. Ladies! It is not okay for a man to hit you -- EVER!! NEVER!!<br /><br />4 -- No condoms. This guy is a whore-dog. Nope! Again. Ladies! Protect yourselves. Condoms. EVERY. Time.<br /><br />There are probably a few other things I could note, but won't. I did like the story, but, it is just okay.<br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>

I was really liking the book and it was a solid 4 star read for a good while there, but I eventually got sick of attending Brenna's pity party.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer779097325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15704561365946831663">4.5 AWESOME BADASS BIKER STARS!<br/><br/>Brenna was raised by bikers, her father Poet being the VP of the Ace's Motorcycle Club. It's a lifestyle filled with crudeness, breaking of laws, subservient "ladies" who are cheated on left and right.... A life she did not want for herself. So she decided to break loose, go to college and make something of herself. Little did she know, the community she ran from, and the man she left high and dry, would be her protector five years later.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=f2c879d4da1aa7407ee1f857e5252825_zps202465fb.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386885543i/7473136._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=a5d1bb6b58519f2579f0fc10a166cf88_zpsa807c480.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386885596i/7473182._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Brenna, married wit</span>
  <span id="freeText15704561365946831663" style="display:none">4.5 AWESOME BADASS BIKER STARS!<br><br>Brenna was raised by bikers, her father Poet being the VP of the Ace's Motorcycle Club. It's a lifestyle filled with crudeness, breaking of laws, subservient "ladies" who are cheated on left and right.... A life she did not want for herself. So she decided to break loose, go to college and make something of herself. Little did she know, the community she ran from, and the man she left high and dry, would be her protector five years later.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=f2c879d4da1aa7407ee1f857e5252825_zps202465fb.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386885543i/7473136._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=a5d1bb6b58519f2579f0fc10a166cf88_zpsa807c480.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386885596i/7473182._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brenna, married with a four year-old daughter Trix, is in an abusive relationship with a man she thought could take care of her and give her a life better than that of a MC Club lady. Her husband Tony, a stockbroker providing her with luxuries but beats her for pleasure, was blissfully unaware of her plans to leave him and hole herself up in Ace's Compound. Brenna knew going back would open up old scars with her father...and Dragon, the man she left high and dry.<br><br>When a Dragon sets eyes on the dark hair, dark eyed little girl, he knew she was his. The timing is perfect. Fuck! He's so pissed...and happy she returned. But why now?<br><br>Loved this book. It was gritty but not uber rough. Brenna battles to gain back the love and trust of her father she abandoned and has to explain herself to Dragon. How does she do it without making it sound like he wasn't good enough for her?<br><br>Loved loved loved Dragon. Here he does the one thing biker brothers do NOT do...fuck a brother's daughter. She high-tails it out of there leaving him to worry about the consequences. Then she shows back up! With his kid! I just fell in love with the tough biker brought to his knees by the little girl who calls him "Papa." Yes, he does one BAD move in the book that had me shaking my head in disgust and there's no explaining it away....but I still loved his character. <br><br>The book was a great combination of suspense, emotional tug of war, and a true feeling of coming home...a place where you will always be loved and protected regardless of the past. Devoured the book in a day!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15704561365946831663" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText16072178820848634470" style="display:none"><b>MY RATING: ☆☆☆☆ Stars <br>Craving Constellations (The Aces #1)<br>by Nicole Jacquelyn</b> <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=vd2rth" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405233352i/10367718._SY540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Re-read this getting ready for the release of book 3 which is just around the corner..<br><br><i>I've spent the last 5 years running, and now it seemed I was heading back to where I ran from..</i> <br><br><i>I'd grown up rough..My father belonged to the Aces MC, he was the vice president, they controlled the gun trade, they lived by their own rules - the law of the club, and once you were in, you were in until the day you died..I'd wanted to make something of myself though, so I'd gone away to college..</i><br><br><i>I met</i> <b>Tony</b> <i>in College, he seemed like one of the good guys, we dated, and eventually we married..</i><br><br><b>Everything set him off!!</b><br><br><i>You know I can take a punch, it's not even a big deal normally.</i><br><br>There was honor in being able to take what someone threw at you..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2zhmbg5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434824i/878050.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Every ache, every pain, and bruise reminded me that we had to escape.<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=5afdok" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434824i/878051.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>He would beat the hell out of me</b> - <i>right in front of my four year old daughter..</i><br><br><b>"How is it, that someone can make decision after decision attempting to get away from their past and somehow end up right back where they started?" </b> <br><br><i>Back to Dragon..Back to the man I ran away from 5 years ago..I met him the night he was getting his cut, to becoming an Ace for life..Screwing a members daughter was one of the worst things a brother could do, right up there with being a rat and screwing their old lady..</i><br><br><b>"Fuckin' Brenna..The fuckin bitch had kept my kid from me!! Fuckin' gone for five fuckin' years..No one hears from you..Now you come back, and I find you had my daughter and didn't tell me "FOR FIVE FUCKIN YEARS!" "Some other guy has been playing daddy to my fuckin daughter!"</b><br><br>This book had it all, love, family unity, loss (DRACON), domestic violence, gang life..<br><br>Anyone who is into sexy bad-ass bikers will LOVE this book, guarantee it..highly recommend..<br><br>You name it, it was all covered in this book, sounds dark but it was so beautifully written that not once did I feel it was a dark read..</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('r6kXp7pZuYrZI3KD/eqzm8OEwzgSLExyoCDbehFt3H8bQm7LMuwanLitNwzeyu/Yp3Hua4a0pwG13iYAxjlEcQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WH3nPsNQF3i4vwHzIKo4voX79vPunNgin/Xco6+s2XLslp5SS+W0btkxRHwDimT94Q7boHoEM1GKCyHZePhBfA==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer14969502682380157938">Nicole Jacquelyn is the mom of two little girls and a full time college student. She hasn’t watched television in well over a year, she still does things that drive her mother crazy, and she loves to read. At eight years old, when asked what she wanted to be when she grew up, she told people she wanted to be a mom. When she was twelve her answer changed- to author. By the time she was eighteen, wh</span>
  <span id="freeText14969502682380157938" style="display:none">Nicole Jacquelyn is the mom of two little girls and a full time college student. She hasn’t watched television in well over a year, she still does things that drive her mother crazy, and she loves to read. At eight years old, when asked what she wanted to be when she grew up, she told people she wanted to be a mom. When she was twelve her answer changed- to author. By the time she was eighteen, when people asked her what she wanted to do with her life, she told them she really wanted to be a writer- but the odds of that happening were so slim that she’d get her business degree “just to be safe”. Her dreams stayed constant. First she became a mom, then she went to college, and during her senior year- with one daughter in first grade and the other in preschool, she sat down and wrote a story.</span>
